(6 comments)

Sorry to be so fussy... batch build scripts need to have very robust error handling. When an error does occur you usually want to stop processing immediately and return a non-zero status. Usually running with '-e' and 'pipefail' is the best approach.

Nothing is more frustrating than spending hours trying to see what happened when you realize that you are just looking at is just a symptom and real cause of the problem occurred 1000 lines earlier.</pre><strong>Reviewer</strong>: Hyperledger Jobbuilder - jobbuilder@jenkins.hyperledger.org<br><strong>Reviewed</strong>: 9/4/2018, 11:15:38 PM<br><strong>Message</strong>: <pre>Patch Set 1: Code-Review-1
